< Text>
DO NOT TAKE YOUR VEHICLE TO THIS SHOP!!!. They take advantage of their customers. Even though my repair was done through an insurance claim, I received my vehicle back to me with dust throughout the car, broken interior panels, broken runner boards, damaged interior door panels, and property damage to my subwoofers (damaged cone and ripped surround). Upon questioning the work performed, employees lied to me about removing interior panels and damaging them. As one who has worked in the automotive industry for 8 years, I could see through these lies. <text>I've been a faithful 24 hour fitness member for as long as I can possibly remember, but I was looking to try out new places in an effort to break away and try something n.

EOS fitness is a fairly new gym that has amazing prices. If you live near their gym, I can see this as being a practical alternative to LA and 24 hour fitness. I went for a 7-day pass and had very little complaints regarding the layout and machines.

During covid, they have a touchless check in. You can either use their keychain ID or your cellphone. You will need a reservation up to 24 hours in advance and the cool part is you can do either 1 or 2 hour reservations.

Cleanliness isn't really all there during this pandemic which is why they get 4 stars from me. There's minimal signage to encourage social distancing so people just assume that every machine is open. News flash: it isn't. But they don't have people monitoring or sanitizing as well so it's a huge free for all and Petri dish.

Still, I'd be willing to give it another shot as I am intrigued by their sauna and other amenities. Overall, I'd consider this to be a great value for those who want to work out and I believe their highest tier is only $25/mo which includes buddy privileges. Always a benefit.

Oh yeah... one thing I wanted to add is that their sales team is terrible. I only got 1 text throughout my 7 day trial asking for assistance on how to get signed up for their membership.< /text>< pics>

< Text>
What an amazing find!!!  We stopped in for breakfast just to kill time between appointments and wow are we glad we did.  We ordered their omelete and their bacon egg potatoe breakfast.  Wilbur ( my husband musician Greg) said the omelete was the absolute best he had ever had, beats even the omelete he covets in Pismo!!  I had the eggs bacon and potatoes.  Eggs were a perfect over medium, bacon crisp and delicious and the poatoes, oh my gosh!!  Sweet potatoes, red potatoes and a wonderful purple potatoe I have never experienced before.  All cut country style and lightly seasoned so you can enjoy the true flavor.  Service was amazing, coffee excelent and the price is well below what we should have paid for such an excellent meal and experience.  Even more surprising they have take out plus you can get delivery through Grub Hub and Door Dash.  Thank you Faguzzi's!  We will be back!!< /Text>
